	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pTypeSalut] == 3)
	{
		new Float:x,Float:a,Float:s;
		GetObjectPos(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]], x,a,s);
		CreateExplosion(x,a,s, 11, 0.8);
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] > 0 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] <= 9) DestroyObject(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]]),PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]] = 0;
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pTypeSalut] == 3 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] == 9) DestroyObject(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutID]),SetPVarInt(playerid,"Salut",0),PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutID] = 0;
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pTypeSalut] == 4)
	{
		new Float:x,Float:a,Float:s;
		GetObjectPos(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]], x,a,s);
		CreateExplosion(x,a,s, 11, 0.8);
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] > 0 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] <= 14) DestroyObject(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]]),PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]] = 0;
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pTypeSalut] == 4 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] == 14) DestroyObject(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutID]),SetPVarInt(playerid,"Salut",0),PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutID] = 0;
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pTypeSalut] == 5)
	{
		new Float:x,Float:a,Float:s;
		GetObjectPos(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]], x,a,s);
		CreateExplosion(x,a,s, 11, 0.8);
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] > 0 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] <= 25) DestroyObject(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]]),PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutes][PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS]] = 0;
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pTypeSalut] == 5 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pStopS] == 25) DestroyObject(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutID]),SetPVarInt(playerid,"Salut",0),PlayerInfo[playerid][pSalutID] = 0;
	}
	return 1;
}
stock DeleteEat(playerid)
{
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pEat] >= 1)
	{
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pEat] = 0;
		if(IsPlayerAttachedObjectSlotUsed(playerid,5)) RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 5);
		SetPlayerSpecialAction(playerid, 0);
	}
}
stock ShiftCords(style, &Float:x, &Float:y, &Float:z, Float:a, Float:distance)
{
	switch(style)
	{
		case 0:
		{
			x += (distance * floatsin(-a, degrees));
			y += (distance * floatcos(-a, degrees));
		}
		case 1:
		{
			x -= (distance * floatsin(-a, degrees));
			y -= (distance * floatcos(-a, degrees));
		}
		default: return 0;
	}
	return 1;
}
stock SetNumber(vidos)
{
	new one,two,text[3][2],twi;
	one = random(9);
	two = random(9);
	twi = random(9);
	new nomer[36],rndtext;
	rndtext = random(20);
	switch(rndtext)
	{
		case 1: text[0] = "a";
		case 2: text[0] = "b";
		case 3: text[0] = "c";
		case 4: text[0] = "d";
		case 5: text[0] = "e";
		case 6: text[0] = "r";
		case 7: text[0] = "t";
		case 8: text[0] = "y";
		case 9: text[0] = "u";
		case 10: text[0] = "q";
		case 11: text[0] = "s";
		case 12: text[0] = "x";
		case 13: text[0] = "z";
		case 14: text[0] = "f";
		case 15: text[0] = "g";
		case 16: text[0] = "h";
		case 17: text[0] = "j";
		case 18: text[0] = "n";
		case 19: text[0] = "b";
		case 20: text[0] = "p";
	}
	rndtext = random(20);
	switch(rndtext)
	{
		case 1: text[1] = "a";
		case 2: text[1] = "b";
		case 3: text[1] = "c";
		case 4: text[1] = "d";
		case 5: text[1] = "e";
		case 6: text[1] = "r";
		case 7: text[1] = "t";
		case 8: text[1] = "y";
		case 9: text[1] = "u";
		case 10: text[1] = "q";
		case 11: text[1] = "s";
		case 12: text[1] = "x";
		case 13: text[1] = "z";
		case 14: text[1] = "f";
		case 15: text[1] = "g";
		case 16: text[1] = "h";
		case 17: text[1] = "j";
		case 18: text[1] = "n";
		case 19: text[1] = "b";
		case 20: text[1] = "p";
	}
	rndtext = random(20);
	switch(rndtext)
	{
		case 1: text[2] = "a";
		case 2: text[2] = "b";
		case 3: text[2] = "c";
		case 4: text[2] = "d";
		case 5: text[2] = "e";
		case 6: text[2] = "r";
		case 7: text[2] = "t";
		case 8: text[2] = "y";
		case 9: text[2] = "u";
		case 10: text[2] = "q";
		case 11: text[2] = "s";
		case 12: text[2] = "x";
		case 13: text[2] = "z";
		case 14: text[2] = "f";
		case 15: text[2] = "g";
		case 16: text[2] = "h";
		case 17: text[2] = "j";
		case 18: text[2] = "n";
		case 19: text[2] = "b";
		case 20: text[2] = "p";
	}
	format(nomer,sizeof(nomer), "%s%d%d%d%s%s",text[0],one,two,twi,text[1],text[2]);
	if(vidos>=LSPDcars[0]||vidos<=LSPDcars[1]||vidos>=FBI[0]||vidos<=FBI[1]||
	vidos>=LVPD[0]||vidos<=LVPD[1]||vidos>=SFPD[0]||vidos<=SFPD[1]) format(nomer,sizeof(nomer), "{0000FF}%s%d%d%d%s%s",text[0],one,two,twi,text[1],text[2]);
	if(IsMOCar(vidos)) format(nomer,sizeof(nomer), "{000000}%s%d%d%d%s%s",text[0],one,two,twi,text[1],text[2]);
	if(IsBusID(vidos) || IsTaxi(vidos) || IsAir(vidos)) format(nomer,sizeof(nomer), "{00FF66}%s%d%d%d%s%s",text[0],one,two,twi,text[1],text[2]);
	SetVehicleNumberPlate(vidos,nomer);
	return 1;
}

f_public DrugsEffect(playerid)
{
	SetPlayerDrunkLevel(playerid, 0);
	SetPlayerWeather(playerid, 0);
	SetPVarInt(playerid,"DrugsEffect",0);
	SetPlayerSpecialAction(playerid, SPECIAL_ACTION_NONE);
 	return 1;
}
f_public F_OnPlayerConnect(playerid)
{
	SetTimerEx("Update", 5, 1, "i", playerid);
	SetTimerEx("Leker", 5, 1, "i", playerid);
 	return 1;
}
f_public Leker(playerid)
{
	if(GetPlayerAmmo(playerid) != loszer[playerid])
	{
		loszer[playerid] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	}
}
f_public Update(playerid)
{
	{
		if(loszer[playerid] == GetPlayerAmmo(playerid))
		{
			Lott[playerid] = false;
		}
		if(loszer[playerid] > GetPlayerAmmo(playerid) && weap[playerid] == GetPlayerWeapon(playerid))
		{
			loszer[playerid] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
			Lott[playerid] = true;
			if(Lott[playerid] == true)
			{
				CallLocalFunction("OnPlayerShoot", "iii", playerid, weap[playerid], loszer[playerid]);
			}
		}
	}
}
f_public OnPlayerShoot( playerid, weaponid, ammo )
{
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 24) PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 25) PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 29) PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 30) PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 31) PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 34) PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo] -= ammo -= PlayerInfo[playerid][pOldAmmo];
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 24) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][2] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo]-1;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 24 && weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][2] <= 0) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][2] = 0;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 25) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][3] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo]-1;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 25 && weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][3] <= 0) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][3] = 0;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 29) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][4] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo]-1;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 29 && weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][4] <= 0) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][4] = 0;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 30) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][5] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo]-1;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 30 && weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][5] <= 0) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][5] = 0;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 31) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][5] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo]-1;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 31 && weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][5] <= 0) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][5] = 0;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 34) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][6] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pNewAmmo]-1;
	if(GetPlayerWeapon(playerid) == 34 && weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][6] <= 0) weapon_anti_cheat[playerid][6] = 0;
 	return 1;
}
f_public F_OnPlayerKeyStateChange(playerid, newkeys, oldkeys)
{
	if(PRESSED(KEY_FIRE))
	{
		loszer[playerid] = GetPlayerAmmo(playerid);
		weap[playerid] = GetPlayerWeapon(playerid);
	}
  	return 1;
}
f_public DiceOff()
{
    foreach(Player, i)
	{
        if(hands_down[i] == 1) hands_down[i] = 0; 
    	if(IsPlayerAttachedObjectSlotUsed(i,1)) RemovePlayerAttachedObject(i,1);
    	ClearAnimations(i);
	}
}
public OnPlayerSelectObject(playerid, type, objectid, modelid, Float:fX, Float:fY, Float:fZ)
{
    new string[80];
    format(string, sizeof(string), "ID объекта: %d\nКоординаты объекта: %f,%f,%f", modelid,fX,fY,fZ);
    ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, 11, DIALOG_STYLE_MSGBOX, "{ffcf00}Редактор", string ,"Изменить", "Удалить");
    SetPVarInt(playerid, "SelectedObject", objectid);
    return 1;
}
public OnPlayerEditObject(playerid, playerobject, objectid, response, Float:fX, Float:fY, Float:fZ, Float:fRotX, Float:fRotY, Float:fRotZ)
{
	if(!playerobject)
	{
		if(!IsValidObject(objectid)) return 1;
		MoveObject(objectid, fX, fY, fZ, 10.0, fRotX, fRotY, fRotZ);
	}
	if(response == EDIT_RESPONSE_FINAL)
	{
		printf("Ид обьекта %d коорды по X %f коорды по Y %f коорды по Z %f",objectid,fX, fY, fZ);
	}
	return 1;
}
f_public Elevator_Boost(floorid)
{
	MoveObject(Obj_Elevator, 1786.678100, -1303.459472, GetElevatorZCoordForFloor(floorid), ELEVATOR_SPEED);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0], X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.459472, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), ELEVATOR_SPEED);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[1], X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.459472, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), ELEVATOR_SPEED);
 	return 1;
}
f_public Elevator_TurnToIdle()
{
	ElevatorState = ELEVATOR_STATE_IDLE;
	ReadNextFloorInQueue();
 	return 1;
}
f_public OnAllMembersLoaded(showid)
{
    new totalMembers = cache_num_rows();
	if(totalMembers > 0)
	{
	    new string[64], bigstring[768];
	    new level, rank, membername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME+1];
		if(strlen(bigstring) < 1) strcat(bigstring, "{DCDCDC}Уровень\tРанг\tИмя\n\n{FFFFFF}");
		for(new i = 0; i < totalMembers; i++)
		{
		    level = cache_get_field_content_int(i, "level", dbHandle);
		    rank = cache_get_field_content_int(i, "rang", dbHandle);
		    cache_get_field_content(i, "name", membername, dbHandle);
			format(bigstring, sizeof(bigstring), "%s%i\t%i\t%s\n", bigstring, level, rank, membername);
		}
		format(string, sizeof(string), "{00D600}Всего в организации %i игроков", totalMembers);
		ShowPlayerDialog(showid, 1277, DIALOG_STYLE_MSGBOX, string, bigstring, "Закрыть", "");
	}
	else SendClientMessage(showid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Игроки не найдены");
}
f_public OnAccountsByIPLoaded(showid, ip[])
{
    new totalAccounts = cache_num_rows();
	if(totalAccounts > 0)
	{
	    new string[64], bigstring[768];
	    new accountname[MAX_PLAYER_NAME+1];
		for(new i = 0; i < totalAccounts; i++)
		{
  			cache_get_field_content(i, "name", accountname);
			format(bigstring,sizeof(bigstring), "%s\n%s", bigstring, accountname);
		}
		format(string, sizeof(string), "%s", ip);
		ShowPlayerDialog(showid, 1277, DIALOG_STYLE_MSGBOX, string, bigstring, "Закрыть", "");
	}
	else SendClientMessage(showid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Аккаунты по указанному IP не найдены");
}
f_public CheckPlayerRegistered(playerid)
{
    new rows, fields;
    cache_get_data (rows, fields);
    SendClientMessage(playerid, 0x0087FF65, "{3399FF}Добро пожаловать на Advance RolePlay!");
    if(rows)
    {
        anti_cheat[playerid][pTimerAC] = 30;
        new ipss[21];
        GetPlayerIp(playerid, ipss, sizeof(ipss));
		format(query,sizeof(query),"{FFFFFF}Добро пожаловать на сервер Advance RolePlay\nВаш ник зарегистрирован\n\nЛогин: {66CC33}%s\n{FFFFFF}Введите пароль:", PlayerInfo[playerid][pName], ipss);
		ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,2,DIALOG_STYLE_INPUT,"{66CCFF}Авторизация",query,"Войти","Отмена");
		login_check[playerid] = false;
    }
    else
    {
       	anti_cheat[playerid][pTimerAC] = 999;
		format(query,sizeof(query),"{FFFFFF}Добро пожаловать на сервер Advance RolePlay\nЧтобы начать игру вам необходимо пройти регистрацию\n\nВведите пароль для Вашего аккаунта\nОн будет запрашиваться каждый раз, когда вы заходите на сервер\n\n\t{33E82D}Примечания:\n\t-Пароль может состоять из русских и латинских символов\n\t-Пароль чувствителен к регистру\n\t-Длина пароля от 6-ти до 15-ти символов");
		ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,1,DIALOG_STYLE_INPUT,"{1472FF}Регистрация",query,"Далее", "");
		login_check[playerid] = false;
    }
    return 1;
}
f_public LoadFuel()
{
    new rows, fields;
    cache_get_data (rows, fields, dbHandle);
    if(rows)
    {
        for(new indexsa = 1; indexsa <= rows; indexsa++)
        {
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "FuelX");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "FuelY");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "FuelZ");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bPrice] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Price");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bRentPlata] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "RentPlata");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bGosRent] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "GosRent");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bRentTime] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "RentTime");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bUpdate] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Updates");
            cache_get_field_content(indexsa-1, "Owner", FuelStInfo[indexsa][bOwner], dbHandle, MAX_PLAYER_NAME+1);
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bOwned] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Owned");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bFuel] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Fuel");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bPriceFuel] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "FuelPrice");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bFuelOne] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "FuelOne");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bCash] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Cash");
            FuelStInfo[indexsa][bLock] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Locked");
        	if(FuelStInfo[indexsa][bOwned] == 0)
			{
				new string[128];
				format(string,sizeof(string),"АЗС\n{ffffff}Цена за 10 литров: {ffcb00}%d$\n{ffffff}Заправка продается",FuelStInfo[indexsa][bPriceFuel]);
				FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelInfo] = Create3DTextLabel(string,0x3196FFFF,FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelX], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelY], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelZ],25.0,0,1);
				FuelStInfo[indexsa][bMap] = CreateDynamicMapIcon(FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelX], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelY], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelZ], 47, -1, 0, -1, -1, 70.0);
			}
			if(FuelStInfo[indexsa][bOwned] == 1)
			{
				new string[128];
				if(FuelStInfo[indexsa][bLock] == 0) format(string,sizeof(string),"АЗС\n{ffffff}Владелец: {6bcf00}%s\n{ffffff}Цена за 10 литров: {ffcb00}%d$",FuelStInfo[indexsa][bOwner],FuelStInfo[indexsa][bPriceFuel]);
				if(FuelStInfo[indexsa][bLock] == 1) format(string,sizeof(string),"АЗС\n{ffffff}Владелец: {6bcf00}%s\n{FF6600}Станция закрыта\n{ffffff}Цена за 10 литров: {ffcb00}%d$",FuelStInfo[indexsa][bOwner],FuelStInfo[indexsa][bPriceFuel]);
				FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelInfo] = Create3DTextLabel(string,0x3196FFFF,FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelX], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelY], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelZ],25.0,0,1);
				FuelStInfo[indexsa][bMap] = CreateDynamicMapIcon(FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelX], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelY], FuelStInfo[indexsa][FuelZ], 47, -1, 0, -1, -1, 70.0);
			}
       	    TotalFuelSt ++;
        	CheckFuels(indexsa);
        }
		//printf("АЗС загружено %i. [Длительность загрузки: %d ms]", TotalFuelSt, cache_get_query_exec_time(UNIT_MILLISECONDS));
    }
    return 1;
}

f_public LoadTerr()
{
	TotalGangZones = cache_num_rows();
    if(TotalGangZones)
    {
        for(new indexsa = 1; indexsa <= TotalGangZones; indexsa++)
        {
            GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][0] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "X");
            GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][1] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "Y");
            GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][2] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "XX");
            GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][3] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "YY");
            GZInfo[indexsa][gMemberZone] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Member");
            GZInfo[indexsa][gID] = GangZoneCreate(GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][0], GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][1], GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][2], GZInfo[indexsa][gCoords][3]);
            GangZoneShowForAll(GZInfo[indexsa][gID], GetGangZoneColor(indexsa));

        	CheckGhetto(indexsa);
        }
		//printf("Территорий загружено %i. [Длительность загрузки: %d ms]", TotalGangZones, cache_get_query_exec_time(UNIT_MILLISECONDS));
    }
    return 1;
}
f_public LoadBiz()
{
    new rows, fields;
    cache_get_data (rows, fields, dbHandle);
    if(rows)
    {
        for(new indexsa = 1; indexsa <= rows; indexsa++)
        {
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitX");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitY");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitZ");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitIntX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitIntX");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitIntY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitIntY");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitIntZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitIntZ");

      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitTpY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitTpY");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitTpZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitTpZ");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][ExitTpA] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "ExitTpA");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bPrice] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Price");
            cache_get_field_content(indexsa-1, "Owner", BizInfo[indexsa][bOwner], dbHandle, MAX_PLAYER_NAME+1);
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bInt] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Inter");

      		BizInfo[indexsa][bRentPlata] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "RentPlata");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bRentTime] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "RentTime");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bWorld] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "World");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bProd] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Prod");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bCash] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Cash");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bGosRent] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "GosRent");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bGotoCena] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "GotoCena");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bSellDrugs] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "SellDrugs");
      		BizInfo[indexsa][bSellCena] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "SellCena");
        	SetCBiz(indexsa);
            TotalBusiness ++;
        	CheckBusiness(indexsa);
        }
		//printf("Бизнесов загружено %i. [Длительность загрузки: %d ms]", TotalBusiness, cache_get_query_exec_time(UNIT_MILLISECONDS));
    }
    return 1;
}
f_public LoadPro(createall)
{
    new rows, fields;
    TotalHouse = cache_num_rows();
    cache_get_data (rows, fields, dbHandle);
    if(rows)
    {
        for(new indexsa = 1; indexsa <= rows; indexsa++)
        {
            HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hExitX");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hExitY");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hExitZ");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitIntX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hExitIntX");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitIntY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hExitIntY");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitIntZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hExitIntZ");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][CarX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hCarX");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][CarY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hCarY");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][CarZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hCarZ");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][CarA] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hCarA");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hPrice] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Price");
			cache_get_field_content(indexsa-1, "Owner", HouseInfo[indexsa][hOwner], dbHandle, MAX_PLAYER_NAME+1);
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hInt] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Inter");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hLock] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Locked");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hCar] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Car");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hCarColorOne] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "CarColorOne");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hCarColorTwo] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "CarColorTwo");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hOwned] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Owned");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hUpdate] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Updates");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hClass] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Class");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hRentPlata] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "Renta");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hRentTime] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "RentTime");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][hWorld] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "World");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreX] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hStoreX");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreY] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hStoreY");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreZ] = cache_get_field_content_float(indexsa-1, "hStoreZ");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreMetall] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "hStoreMetall");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreAmmo] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "hStoreAmmo");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreDrugs] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "hStoreDrugs");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreSkin] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "hStoreSkin");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][StoreGun] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "hStoreGun");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pWheels] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pWheels");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pNitro] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pNitro");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pHydrawlic] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pHydrawlic");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pSpoiler] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pSpoiler");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pBumper1] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pBumper1");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pBumper2] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pBumper2");
            HouseInfo[indexsa][pPaintJob] = cache_get_field_content_int(indexsa-1, "pPaintJob");
            if(createall)
            {
        		if(HouseInfo[indexsa][hOwned] == 0)
				{
					HouseInfo[indexsa][hPickup] = CreatePickup(1273, 23, HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitX], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitY], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitZ],-1);
					HouseInfo[indexsa][hMIcon] = CreateDynamicMapIcon(HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitX], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitY], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitZ], 31, -1, 0, -1, -1, 400.0);
				}
				if(HouseInfo[indexsa][hOwned] == 1)
				{
					HouseInfo[indexsa][hPickup] = CreatePickup(19522, 23, HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitX], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitY], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitZ],-1);
					HouseInfo[indexsa][hMIcon] = CreateDynamicMapIcon(HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitX], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitY], HouseInfo[indexsa][ExitZ], 32, -1, 0, -1, -1, 400.0);
				}
				CheckHouse(indexsa);
			}
			if(!createall)
			{
				UpdateHouse(indexsa);
			}
        }
		//printf("[%i] Дома загружены. [Длительность загрузки: %d ms]", TotalHouse, cache_get_query_exec_time(UNIT_MILLISECONDS));
    }
    return 1;
}

f_public sm_hand_back(playerid, objectid, i)
{
	MoveDynamicObject(objectid, sm_hand_coord[i][0], sm_hand_coord[i][1], sm_hand_coord[i][2], 2, sm_hand_coord[i][3], sm_hand_coord[i][4], sm_hand_coord[i][5]);
	i = ((i + 1) * 2 + ((i + 1) - 2)) - 1;
	SetTimerEx("sm_move", 348, false, "id", playerid, i);
	return 1;
}
f_public sm_move (playerid, i)
{
	new Float: obj_pos_z;
	new move_time;
	GetDynamicObjectPos (sm_slot [i], obj_pos_z, obj_pos_z, obj_pos_z);
	if(sm_slot_coord [i] [2] != obj_pos_z)
	{
		move_time = MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i], sm_slot_coord [i] [0], sm_slot_coord [i] [1], sm_slot_coord [i] [2], 0.04, image_rot [random (sizeof (image_rot))],  sm_slot_coord [i] [4], sm_slot_coord [i] [5]);
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i + 1], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [0], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [1], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [2], 0.04, image_rot [random (sizeof (image_rot))], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [4], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [5]);
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i + 2], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [0], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [1], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [2], 0.04, image_rot [random (sizeof (image_rot))], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [4], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [5]);
	}
	else
	{
		move_time = MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i], sm_slot_coord [i] [0], sm_slot_coord [i] [1], sm_slot_coord [i] [2] + 0.02, 0.04, image_rot [random (sizeof (image_rot))],  sm_slot_coord [i] [4], sm_slot_coord [i] [5]);
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i + 1], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [0], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [1], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [2] + 0.02, 0.04, image_rot [random (sizeof (image_rot))], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [4], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [5]);
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i + 2], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [0], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [1], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [2] + 0.02, 0.04, image_rot [random (sizeof (image_rot))], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [4], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [5]);
	}
	SetTimerEx ("sm_check", move_time + 100, false, "iddd", playerid, sm_slot [i], sm_slot [i + 1], sm_slot [i + 2]);
	return 1;
}
f_public sm_check (playerid, obj_1, obj_2, obj_3)
{
	if(GetPVarInt(playerid, "sm_bet") == 0) return 1;
	new result = get_result (obj_1, obj_2, obj_3);
	if(!result)
	{
		PlayerTextDrawSetString(playerid, sm_ptd[playerid], "Stavka: 0$");
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] -= GetPVarInt(playerid, "sm_bet");
		GivePlayerMoney(playerid, - GetPVarInt(playerid, "sm_bet"));
		DeletePVar(playerid, "sm_bet");
	}
	else
	{
		new win_cash = GetPVarInt(playerid, "sm_bet") * (7 - result);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] += win_cash;
		GivePlayerMoney(playerid, win_cash);
		new string[45];
		format(string, sizeof(string), "Поздравляем! Вы выйграли! {59d50f}%d$", win_cash);
		SendClientMessage(playerid,0x9C69FFFF,string);
		PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 4201, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
		DeletePVar(playerid, "sm_bet");
		GameTextForPlayer(playerid, string, 4000, 3);
		format(string, 45, "~y~YOU WIN!~n~~g~+%d$", win_cash);
		GameTextForPlayer(playerid, string, 5000, 3);
		PlayerTextDrawSetString (playerid, sm_ptd [playerid], "Stavka: 0$");
	}
	DeletePVar(playerid, "sm_started");
	return 1;
}
//Калигула времянка
stock get_result ( obj_1, obj_2, obj_3 )
{
    new Float: rot_pos [ 4 ];
    GetDynamicObjectRot ( obj_1, rot_pos [ 0 ], rot_pos [ 3 ], rot_pos [ 3 ] ) ;
    GetDynamicObjectRot ( obj_2, rot_pos [ 1 ], rot_pos [ 3 ], rot_pos [ 3 ] ) ;
    GetDynamicObjectRot ( obj_3, rot_pos [ 2 ], rot_pos [ 3 ], rot_pos [ 3 ] ) ;

    if ( rot_pos [ 0 ] == rot_pos [ 1 ] && rot_pos [ 0 ] == rot_pos [ 2 ] && rot_pos [ 0 ] && rot_pos [ 0 ] == 200 ) return COMBO_DOUBLE_GOLD;
    new combo_points = 0;

    for ( new i = 0; i < sizeof ( cherry_combo ) ; i++ )
    {
        for ( new f = 0; f < sizeof ( rot_pos ) - 1; f++ )
        {
            if ( rot_pos [ f ] == cherry_combo [ i ] )combo_points ++ ;
        }
    }
    if ( combo_points == 3 ) return COMBO_CHERRY;
    combo_points = 0;
    for ( new i = 0; i < sizeof ( gold_combo ) ; i++ )
    {
        for ( new f = 0; f < sizeof ( rot_pos ) - 1; f++ )
        {
            if ( rot_pos [ f ] == gold_combo [ i ] )combo_points ++ ;
        }
    }
    if ( combo_points == 3 ) return COMBO_GOLD;
    combo_points = 0;
    for ( new i = 0; i < sizeof ( bell_combo ) ; i++ )
    {
        for ( new f = 0; f < sizeof ( rot_pos ) - 1; f++ )
        {
            if ( rot_pos [ f ] == bell_combo [ i ] )combo_points ++ ;
        }
    }
    if ( combo_points == 3 ) return COMBO_BELL;
    combo_points = 0;
    for ( new i = 0; i < sizeof ( grapes_combo ) ; i++ )
    {
        for ( new f = 0; f < sizeof ( rot_pos ) - 1; f++ )
        {
            if ( rot_pos [ f ] == grapes_combo [ i ] )combo_points ++ ;
        }
    }
    if ( combo_points == 3 ) return COMBO_GRAPES;
    combo_points = 0;
    for ( new i = 0; i < sizeof ( sn_combo ) ; i++ )
    {
        for ( new f = 0; f < sizeof ( rot_pos ) - 1; f++ )
        {
            if ( rot_pos [ f ] == sn_combo [ i ] )combo_points ++ ;
        }
    }
    if ( combo_points == 3 ) return COMBO_69;
    return false;
}

stock WarnAC(playerid)
{
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pWarn] < 3)
	{
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pWarn] += 1;
		format(query, sizeof(query), "[Античит] %s[%d] получил предупреждение [%i|3].", PlayerInfo[playerid][pName], playerid, PlayerInfo[playerid][pWarn]);
		SendClientMessageToAll(COLOR_LIGHTRED, query);
		SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xff6600AA, "Для снятия предупреждений используйте команду {00cc00}/unwarn");
		SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xff6600AA, "До снятия всех предупреждений Вам запрещено вступать в организации.");
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pRang] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkinOrg] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnWarn] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnWarntest] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSetSpawn] = 0;
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pWarn] == 3)
		{
			new curdate = getdate();
			PlayerInfo[playerid][pBan] = 1;
			PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnBanTime] = curdate+10;
			PlayerInfo[playerid][pWarn] = 0;
		}
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader] >= 1)
		{
		new qser[150];
		format(qser, sizeof(qser), "SELECT * FROM leaders WHERE idorg = '%i'", PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader]);
		new Cache: lololo = mysql_query(dbHandle,qser,true);
		if(cache_num_rows() > 0)
		{
			format(qser, sizeof(qser), "DELETE FROM leaders WHERE idorg = '%i' LIMIT 1", PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader]);
			mysql_pquery(dbHandle,qser);
		}
		cache_delete(lololo);
		}
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader] = 0;
		SetPlayerSkin(playerid,PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin]);
		KickEx(playerid);
	}
	return 1;
}
stock IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, animation[])
{
	if(!GetPlayerAnimationIndex(playerid)) return 0;
	new animlib[32], animname[32];
	GetAnimationName(GetPlayerAnimationIndex(playerid), animlib, sizeof(animlib), animname, sizeof(animname));
	if(!strcmp(animname, animation, true)) return 1;
 	return 0;
}
stock TakeRuda(playerid)
{
	if(PlayerStartJob[playerid] == true)
	{
		if(IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_back")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_collapse")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_fall")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_front")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_glide")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_land")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "FALL_skyDive")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "JUMP_glide")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "JUMP_land")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "JUMP_launch")
				|| IsPlayerApplyAnimation(playerid, "JUMP_launch_R"))
		{
			if(!IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(playerid, 3, -1809.8923,-1646.2524,22.9467)
					&& !IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(playerid, 3, -1811.7421,-1652.0760,22.7451))
			{
				SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF6600AA, "Вы уронили руду.");
				ApplyAnimation(playerid, "CARRY", "crry_prtial", 4.0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1);
				PlayerStartJob[playerid] = false;
				if(IsPlayerAttachedObjectSlotUsed(playerid,4)) RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 4);
				SetPlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 3, 18634, 6, 0.078222, 0.000000, 0.110844, 298.897308, 264.126861, 193.350555, 1.000000, 1.000000, 1.000000);
				GetPlayerMetall[playerid] = 0;
				return 1;
			}
		}
	}
	return 1;
}

}

stock IsMed(playerid)
{
	new model = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
	if(model >= BolkaLSCars[0] || model <= BolkaLSCars[1])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	if(model >= Vert[0] || model <= Vert[1])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	if(model >= SFMZ[0] || model <= SFMZ[1])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	if(model >= LVMZ[0] || model <= LVMZ[1])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}

stock BankLog(playerid,giver,summa)
{
	new daysa,monthsa,yearsa,string[20],playerips[20],saasa[200];
	getdate(yearsa,monthsa,daysa);
	GetPlayerIp(playerid,playerips,sizeof(playerips));
	format(string, sizeof(string), "%d/%d/%d",daysa,monthsa,yearsa);
	format(saasa, sizeof(saasa), "INSERT INTO logsbank (NickGo,NickTo,Summa,Dater,IpGo) VALUES ('%s','%s','%i','%s','%s')",PlayerInfo[playerid][pName], PlayerInfo[giver][pName],summa,string,playerips);
	mysql_pquery(dbHandle, saasa);
	return 1;
}
stock AdminLogChat(text[])
{
	new daysa,monthsa,yearsa,string[20],saasa[200];
	getdate(yearsa,monthsa,daysa);
	format(string, sizeof(string), "%d/%d/%d",daysa,monthsa,yearsa);
	new strtime[20],timeh,timem,times;
	gettime(timeh,timem,times);
	format(strtime, sizeof(strtime), "%d:%d:%d",timeh,timem,times);
	format(saasa, sizeof(saasa), "INSERT INTO adminchat (Text,Dater,Timers) VALUES ('%s','%s','%s')",text,string,strtime);
	mysql_pquery(dbHandle, saasa);
	return 1;
}

stock SaveAll(playerid)
{
	OnPlayerSave(playerid);
	SaveTwo(playerid);
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pFuel] < 999 && login_check[playerid] == true) SaveFuelSt(PlayerInfo[playerid][pFuel]);
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pBusiness] < 999 && login_check[playerid] == true) SaveBiz(PlayerInfo[playerid][pBusiness]);
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse] < 999 && login_check[playerid] == true)
	{
		SaveStoreHouse(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse]);
		SaveHouse(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse]);
	}
	return 1;
}

stock AmmoTake(i)
{
	if(!IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010)) return 1;
	if(PlayerInfo[i][pMember] != 8 && !IsGhettor(i)) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы не можете пользоваться этим складом.");
	if(StoreMO[1][oAmmo] < 0) return StoreMO[1][oAmmo] = 0,UpdateStoresMO();
	if(StoreMO[2][oAmmo] < 0) return StoreMO[2][oAmmo] = 0,UpdateStoresMO();
	if(StoreMO[3][oAmmo] < 0) return StoreMO[3][oAmmo] = 0,UpdateStoresMO();
	if(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) == 50 && IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010))
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[i][pAFK] == false)
		{
			new stringer[20];
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] >= 400 && PlayerInfo[i][pUpdate] < 2) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD, "Вы не можете взять больше патронов."),PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] = 400;
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] >= 1000 && PlayerInfo[i][pUpdate] >= 2) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD, "Вы не можете взять больше патронов."),PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] = 1000;
			if(StoreMO[1][oAmmo] <= 0) StoreMO[1][oAmmo] = 0;
			if(StoreMO[1][oAmmo] <= 0) return 0;
			new ammo = 3,infoammo[24];
			ammo += random(3);
			format(stringer, sizeof(stringer), "+ %d пт.",ammo);
			SetPlayerChatBubble(i, stringer, 0xFFFAFAAA, 5.0, 1000);
			PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] += ammo;
			if(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) == 50 && IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010)) StoreMO[1][oAmmo] -= ammo;
			format(infoammo, sizeof(infoammo), "~b~+%d pt",ammo);
			GameTextForPlayer(i, infoammo, 1000, 4);
			UpdateStoresMO();
		}
	}
	if(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) == 100 && IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010))
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[i][pAFK] == false)
		{
			new stringer[20];
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] >= 400 && PlayerInfo[i][pUpdate] < 2) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD, "Вы не можете взять больше патронов."),PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] = 400;
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] >= 1000 && PlayerInfo[i][pUpdate] >= 2) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD, "Вы не можете взять больше патронов."),PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] = 1000;
			if(StoreMO[2][oAmmo] <= 0) StoreMO[2][oAmmo] = 0;
			if(StoreMO[2][oAmmo] <= 0) return 0;
			new ammo = 3,infoammo[24];
			ammo += random(3);
			format(stringer, sizeof(stringer), "+ %d пт.",ammo);
			SetPlayerChatBubble(i, stringer, 0xFFFAFAAA, 5.0, 1000);
			PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] += ammo;
			if(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) == 100 && IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010)) StoreMO[2][oAmmo] -= ammo;
			format(infoammo, sizeof(infoammo), "~b~+%d pt",ammo);
			GameTextForPlayer(i, infoammo, 1000, 4);
			UpdateStoresMO();
		}
	}
	if(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) == 150 && IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010))
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[i][pAFK] == false)
		{
			new stringer[20];
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] >= 400 && PlayerInfo[i][pUpdate] < 2) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD, "Вы не можете взять больше патронов."),PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] = 400;
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] >= 1000 && PlayerInfo[i][pUpdate] >= 2) return SendClientMessage(i,COLOR_GRAD, "Вы не можете взять больше патронов."),PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] = 1000;
			if(StoreMO[3][oAmmo] <= 0) StoreMO[3][oAmmo] = 0;
			if(StoreMO[3][oAmmo] <= 0) return 0;
			new ammo = 3,infoammo[24];
			ammo += random(3);
			format(stringer, sizeof(stringer), "+ %d пт.",ammo);
			SetPlayerChatBubble(i, stringer, 0xFFFAFAAA, 5.0, 1000);
			PlayerInfo[i][pAmmo] += ammo;
			if(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) == 150 && IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(i,2.0,311.7813,-165.9848,999.6010)) StoreMO[3][oAmmo] -= ammo;
			format(infoammo, sizeof(infoammo), "~b~+%d pt",ammo);
			GameTextForPlayer(i, infoammo, 1000, 4);
			UpdateStoresMO();
		}
	}
	PlayerInfo[i][pTimer] = 2;
	return 1;
}
stock MySQLConnect()
{
 	printf("DOOME CONNECT - Идёт подключение к базе данных: %s", MySQLSettings[DOOME_USERNAME]);
	printf("Подождите, пожалуйста, идёт загрузка . . .");
    dbHandle = mysql_connect(MySQLSettings[DOOME_HOST],MySQLSettings[DOOME_USERNAME],MySQLSettings[DOOME_DATABASE],MySQLSettings[DOOME_PASSWORD]);//Подключение к базе данных и объявление её переменной dbHandle
    if(mysql_errno() == 0)
    {
    	printf("Подключение MySQL: Удачно.");
    }
    else
    {
    	printf("Подключение MySQL: Не удалось.");
    }
    mysql_query(dbHandle, "SET NAMES cp1251", false);//Придаём именам необходимый формат для записи в базу
    return 1;
}

		if(BizInfo[h][bClass] == 34 && BizInfo[h][bLock] == 0) format(string,sizeof(string),"Автомастерская\n{FFFFFF}Владелец: {0099FF}%s\n{0099FF}Бизнес открыт",BizInfo[h][bOwner]);
		if(BizInfo[h][bClass] == 34 && BizInfo[h][bLock] == 1) format(string,sizeof(string),"Автомастерская\n{FFFFFF}Владелец: {0099FF}%s\n{FF6600}Бизнес закрыт",BizInfo[h][bOwner]);
		BizInfo[h][Text] = Create3DTextLabel(string,0xFFFF00FF,BizInfo[h][ExitX], BizInfo[h][ExitY], BizInfo[h][ExitZ]+1,15.0,0,1);
		if(BizInfo[h][bClass] == 1) BizInfo[h][bPickupMagaz] = CreatePickup(2663, 2, -29.0224,-185.1309,1003.5469,BizInfo[h][bWorld]);
		if(BizInfo[h][bClass] == 13) BizInfo[h][Hippy] = Create3DTextLabel(hippys,COLOR_WHITE,273.9077,305.0173,1000.1484,15.0,BizInfo[h][bWorld],1);
	}
}

stock CheckAccount(playerid)
{
	new plrIP[16];
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pInGameTime] > 60) PlayerInfo[playerid][pInGameTime] = 1;
	GetPlayerIp(playerid, plrIP, sizeof(plrIP));
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pLastIP] = plrIP;
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pScodetest] == 1)
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pRegIP] == PlayerInfo[playerid][pLastIP])
		{
			login_check[playerid] = true;
			TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 1);
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pBan] == 1)
			{
				new stringe[200];
				new curdate11 = getdate();
				new ostalos=PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnBanTime]-curdate11;
				if(ostalos <= 0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pBan] = 0;
				if(ostalos <= 0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnBanTime] = 0;
				format(stringe,sizeof(stringe),"{FFFFFF}Данный аккаунт заблокирован на {0099FF}%i{FFFFFF} дней.\n{FFFFFF}Введите {00FFFF}/q {FFFFFF}чтобы выйти.", ostalos);
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pBan] == 1) ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,1277,DIALOG_STYLE_MSGBOX,"{0066FF}Advance RolePlay",stringe,"Закрыть","");
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pBan] == 1) KickEx(playerid);
			}
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnWarntest] == 1)
			{
				new curdates = getdate();
				new os=PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnWarn]-curdates;
				if(os <= 0)
				{
					PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnWarntest] = 0;
					PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnWarn] = 0;
					PlayerInfo[playerid][pWarn] = 0;
				}
			}
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pBan] == 0)
			{
				new pname2[36];
				GetPlayerName(playerid, pname2, 36);
				warpass[playerid] = 0;
				SetPlayerWantedLevel(playerid,PlayerInfo[playerid][pWanted]);
				switch(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember])
				{
					case 10: SetPlayerFightingStyle(playerid,FIGHT_STYLE_KNEEHEAD);
					case 11: SetPlayerFightingStyle(playerid,FIGHT_STYLE_KUNGFU);
					case 12: SetPlayerFightingStyle(playerid,FIGHT_STYLE_BOXING);
				}
				switch(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLevel])
				{
					case 1: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1760.7727,-1903.9078,13.5655,271.3320, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 2: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1760.7727,-1903.9078,13.5655,271.3320, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 3: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1199.4821,-1759.9143,13.5850,83.8091, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 4: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1199.4821,-1759.9143,13.5850,83.8091, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 5: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], -1968.0267,159.8920,27.6875,180.6863, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 6: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], -1968.0267,159.8920,27.6875,180.6863, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 7: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], -1968.0267,159.8920,27.6875,180.6863, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					case 8: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], -1968.0267,159.8920,27.6875,180.6863, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
				}
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLevel] < 5)
				{
					new rndsp;
					rndsp = random(4);
					if(rndsp == 0) rndsp = 2;
					if(rndsp == 1) SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1760.7727,-1903.9078,13.5655,271.3320, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					if(rndsp == 2) SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1199.4821,-1759.9143,13.5850,83.8091, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					if(rndsp == 3) SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1755.8176,-1900.3982,13.5625,264.4793, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
					if(rndsp == 4) SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin], 1197.8406,-1764.5494,13.5842,70.4866, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
				}
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLevel] >= 9) SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 255, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkinOrg], 2838.5291,1303.5842,11.3906,93.8858, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse] < 999 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pSetSpawn] == 15)
				{
					SetPlayerInterior(playerid,HouseInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse]][hInt]);

				}
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSetSpawn] == 1)

				}

				CompVeh(playerid,caridhouse[playerid]);
				VehicleFuel[caridhouse[playerid]] = fuelplease;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pEngine] = 0;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pLights] = 0;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pAlarm] = 0;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pDoors] = 1;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBonnet] = 0;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBoot] = 0;
				VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pObjective] = 0;
				SetVehicleParamsEx(caridhouse[playerid],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pEngine],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pLights],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pAlarm],1,VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBonnet],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBoot],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pObjective]);
			}
		}
	}
}

stock BanIP(ip[], days)
{
	new mquery[255];
	mysql_format(dbHandle, mquery, sizeof(mquery), "INSERT INTO ip_bans (ip_ban_address, ip_ban_date, ip_ban_expdate) VALUES ('%e', NOW(), NOW() + INTERVAL %d DAY)", ip, days);
	mysql_pquery(dbHandle, mquery);
	return 1;
}
stock IsIPBanned(ip[])
{
	new mquery[255], bool:isBanned;
	isBanned = false;
	mysql_format(dbHandle, mquery, sizeof(mquery), "SELECT * FROM ip_bans WHERE ip_ban_address = '%e' AND ip_ban_expdate > NOW() LIMIT 1", ip);
	new Cache: resultCache = mysql_query(dbHandle, mquery, true);
	if(cache_num_rows() > 0) isBanned = true;
	cache_delete(resultCache);
	return isBanned;
}
stock UnBanIP(ip[])
{
	new mquery[255];
	mysql_format(dbHandle, mquery, sizeof(mquery), "DELETE FROM ip_bans WHERE ip_ban_address = '%e' LIMIT 1", ip);
	mysql_pquery(dbHandle, mquery);
}
stock strreplace(string[], find, replace)
{
	for(new i=0; string[i]; i++)
 	{
  		if(string[i] == find)
        {
        	string[i] = replace;
        }
	}
}
stock GetTimeCp()
{
	new infotimecapture;
	gettime(infotimecapture);
	if(infotimecapture >= 13 && infotimecapture <= 23)
	{
	    return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}
stock GetTimeAf()
{
	new infotimecapture;
	gettime(infotimecapture);
	if(infotimecapture >= 14 && infotimecapture <= 23)
	{
	    return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}
stock WriteLog(logname[], message[])
{
	new tmphour, tmpminute, tmpsecond, tmpyear, tmpmonth, tmpday, string[512];
	new File: log = fopen(logname, io_append);

	gettime(tmphour, tmpminute, tmpsecond);
	getdate(tmpyear, tmpmonth, tmpday);

	format(string, sizeof(string), "[%02d:%02d:%02d][%02d/%02d/%d] %s\n", tmphour, tmpminute, tmpsecond, tmpday, tmpmonth, tmpyear, message);
	fwrite(log, string);
	fclose(log);
}

stock ShowPDD(playerid)
{
	new string[3400];
	format(string,sizeof(string),"{0099FF}Глава 1: Основные правила.{ffffff}\n");
	strcat(string, "1. Настоящие Правила дорожного движения (ПДД) устанавливают\nединый порядок дорожного движения на всей территории San Andreas.\n2. Обгон транспортного средства разрешен только с левой\nстороны, при этом водитель обязан убедиться, что встречная\nполоса свободна на достаточном, для обгона, расстоянии.\n", sizeof(string));
	strcat(string, "3. При ДТП водители обязаны вызвать полицию и дождаться приезда ДПС.\n4. При виде ДПС с включенной сиреной,водитель обязан замедлить скорость и прижаться к обочине.\n", sizeof(string));
    strcat(string, "5. Водитель обязан предъявить документы патрульному, если тот попросит.\n\n{0099FF}Глава 2: Скорость движения.{ffffff}\n1. В пределах города разрешается движение транспортных\nсредств со скоростью не более 60 км/ч.\n2. В жилых зонах и дворовых териториях не более 30 км/ч.\n3. За городом скоростных ограничений нет.\n\n{0099FF}Глава 3: Остановка и стоянка\n{ffffff}1. Остановка и стоянка разрешены на обочине, если нет запрещающих знаков.", sizeof(string));
    strcat(string, "\n2. Парковка разрешена в специально отведенных для этого местах.\n\n{0099FF}Глава 4: Управление.{ffffff}\n1. Чтобы завести автомобиль, нажмите left ctrl или используйте команду \"/e\".\n2. Чтобы включить фары, нажмите left alt или используйте команду \"/l\".\n3. Чтобы снять ограничитель скорости, нажмите NUM4 или \"/sl\".\n4. Чтобы заправиться на АЗС, нажмите NUM2 или \"/i\".\n\n{0099FF}Глава 5: Информация об автомобиле.{ffffff}", sizeof(string));
    strcat(string, "\n1. Объем бензобака - 150 литров.\n2. Время работы при полном баке - 2 часа. (Чтобы сохранить\nколличество бензина в баке, выключайте двигатель, так топливо\nбудет расходоваться медленнее.)\n3. Кол-во HP автомобиля - 1000.{0099FF}\n\nГлава 6: Теоретическая часть.{ffffff}\n1. Если перед Вами на дорогу выбежал человек, нужно немедленно остановиться\n и пропустить его.\n2. Если вы поворачиваете налево, нужно пропустить все\nавтомобили, едущие Вам навстречу.", sizeof(string));
    strcat(string, "\n3. Если Ваш автомобиль сломается, нужно остановиться, включить\nгабариты и вызвать механика.{FFCC00}\n\nЖелаем удачи на экзамене!", sizeof(string));
	ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,1277,DIALOG_STYLE_MSGBOX,"{FFFAFA}Автошкола",string,"Закрыть","");
	return 1;
}
stock CheckVibori(playerid,pickupid)
{
	new azaza[200];
	if(pickupid == bulleten)
	{
		if(votestart == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,0xFF6600AA, "Голосование закрыто.");
		if(bullet[playerid] == true) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_WHITE, "У вас есть бюллетень.");
		if(golos[playerid] == true) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы уже голосовали.");
		bullet[playerid] = true;
		SendClientMessage(playerid,0x00cc00AA, "Вы взяли бюллетень.");
	}
	if(pickupid == bull1)
	{
		if(votestart == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,0xFF6600AA, "Голосование закрыто.");
		if(bullet[playerid] == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_WHITE, "У вас нет бюллетени.");
		if(golos[playerid] == true) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы уже голосовали.");
		format(azaza, sizeof(azaza), "Кандидат №1:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s\nКандидат №2:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s\nКандидат №3:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s",candidate1,party1,candidate2,party2,candidate3,party3);
		ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,261,DIALOG_STYLE_LIST,"Кандидаты на выборы президента",azaza,"Голос","Закрыть");
	}
	if(pickupid == bull2)
	{
		if(votestart == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,0xFF6600AA, "Голосование закрыто.");
		if(bullet[playerid] == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_WHITE, "У вас нет бюллетени.");
		if(golos[playerid] == true) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы уже голосовали.");
		format(azaza, sizeof(azaza), "Кандидат №1:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s\nКандидат №2:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s\nКандидат №3:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s",candidate1,party1,candidate2,party2,candidate3,party3);
		ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,261,DIALOG_STYLE_LIST,"Кандидаты на выборы президента",azaza,"Голос","Закрыть");
	}
	if(pickupid == bull3)
	{
		if(votestart == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,0xFF6600AA, "Голосование закрыто.");
		if(bullet[playerid] == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_WHITE, "У вас нет бюллетени.");
		if(golos[playerid] == true) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы уже голосовали.");
		format(azaza, sizeof(azaza), "Кандидат №1:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s\nКандидат №2:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s\nКандидат №3:\t{CCFF00}%s{ffffff} | %s",candidate1,party1,candidate2,party2,candidate3,party3);
		ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,261,DIALOG_STYLE_LIST,"Кандидаты на выборы президента",azaza,"Голос","Закрыть");
	}
	return 1;
}
stock Checkadmin_combo(playerid)
{
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] > 0)
	{
	    if(admin_combo[playerid][pTimer] > 0)
	    {
			if(admin_combo[playerid][pJail] > 4 || admin_combo[playerid][pWarn] > 4 || admin_combo[playerid][pBan] > 3 || admin_combo[playerid][pKick] > 4 || admin_combo[playerid][pSKick] > 5 || admin_combo[playerid][pMute] > 4 || admin_combo[playerid][pRban] > 3 || admin_combo[playerid][pUnRban] > 3 || admin_combo[playerid][pMsg] > 6 || admin_combo[playerid][pSBan] > 2)
			{
	        	PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] = 0;
	        	SaveAll(playerid);
	        	new string[128];
	        	format(string, sizeof(string), "[A] %s[%d] был снят с поста администратора системой безопасности. Возможно взломан",PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],playerid);
	        	SMA(5,0xFF0000AA, string);
	        	clear_admin_combo(playerid);
	        }
		}
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader] > 0)
	{
	    if(admin_combo[playerid][pTimer] > 0)
	    {
			if(admin_combo[playerid][pNews] > 5)
			{
			 	new string[128];
	        	format(string, sizeof(string), "[A] %s[%d] был снят с поста лидера системой безопасности. Возможно взломан",PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],playerid);
	        	SMA(5,0xFF0000AA, string);
	        	WarnAC(playerid);
	        	SaveAll(playerid);
	        	clear_admin_combo(playerid);
	        }
		}
	}
}
stock clear_admin_combo(playerid)
{
    admin_combo[playerid][pJail] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pWarn] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pBan] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pKick] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pSKick] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pMute] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pRban] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pUnban] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pUnRban] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pMsg] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pSBan] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pNews] = 0;
    admin_combo[playerid][pTimer] = 0;
}

stock ShowElevatorDialog(playerid)
{
	new string[512];
	for(new i; i < sizeof(ElevatorQueue); i ++)
	{
		if(FloorRequestedBy[i] != INVALID_PLAYER_ID)
		strcat(string, "{FF0000}");
		strcat(string, FloorNames[i]);
		strcat(string, "\n");
	}
	ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, 8, DIALOG_STYLE_LIST, "{4682B4}Лифт телецентра", string, "Пуск", "Отмена");
 	return 1;
}
stock Elevator_Initialize()
{
	Obj_Elevator = CreateObject(18755, 1786.678100, -1303.459472, GROUND_Z_COORD + ELEVATOR_OFFSET, 0.000000, 0.000000, 270.000000);
	Obj_ElevatorDoors[0] = CreateObject(18757, X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.459472, GROUND_Z_COORD, 0.000000, 0.000000, 270.000000);
	Obj_ElevatorDoors[1] = CreateObject(18756, X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.459472, GROUND_Z_COORD, 0.000000, 0.000000, 270.000000);
	for(new i; i < sizeof(Obj_FloorDoors); i ++)
	{
		Obj_FloorDoors[i][0] = CreateObject(18757, X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.171142, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(i), 0.000000, 0.000000, 270.000000);
		Obj_FloorDoors[i][1] = CreateObject(18756, X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.171142, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(i), 0.000000, 0.000000, 270.000000);
	}
	Floor_OpenDoors(0);
	Elevator_OpenDoors();
 	return 1;
}
stock Elevator_Destroy()
{
	DestroyObject(Obj_Elevator);
	DestroyObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0]);
	DestroyObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[1]);
	for(new i; i < sizeof(Obj_FloorDoors); i ++)
	{
		DestroyObject(Obj_FloorDoors[i][0]);
		DestroyObject(Obj_FloorDoors[i][1]);
	}
 	return 1;
}
stock Elevator_OpenDoors()
{
	new Float:x, Float:y, Float:z;
	GetObjectPos(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0], x, y, z);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0], X_DOOR_L_OPENED, y, z, DOORS_SPEED);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[1], X_DOOR_R_OPENED, y, z, DOORS_SPEED);
 	return 1;
}
stock Elevator_CloseDoors()
{
	if(ElevatorState == ELEVATOR_STATE_MOVING)
 	return 0;
	new Float:x, Float:y, Float:z;
	GetObjectPos(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0], x, y, z);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0], X_DOOR_CLOSED, y, z, DOORS_SPEED);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[1], X_DOOR_CLOSED, y, z, DOORS_SPEED);
 	return 1;
}
stock Floor_OpenDoors(floorid)
{
    PlayerPlaySound(floorid, 6401, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
	MoveObject(Obj_FloorDoors[floorid][0], X_DOOR_L_OPENED, -1303.171142, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), DOORS_SPEED);
	MoveObject(Obj_FloorDoors[floorid][1], X_DOOR_R_OPENED, -1303.171142, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), DOORS_SPEED);
 	return 1;
}
stock Floor_CloseDoors(floorid)
{
	MoveObject(Obj_FloorDoors[floorid][0], X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.171142, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), DOORS_SPEED);
	MoveObject(Obj_FloorDoors[floorid][1], X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.171142, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), DOORS_SPEED);
 	return 1;
}
stock Elevator_MoveToFloor(floorid)
{
	ElevatorState = ELEVATOR_STATE_MOVING;
	ElevatorFloor = floorid;
	MoveObject(Obj_Elevator, 1786.678100, -1303.459472, GetElevatorZCoordForFloor(floorid), 0.5);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[0], X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.459472, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), 0.5);
	MoveObject(Obj_ElevatorDoors[1], X_DOOR_CLOSED, -1303.459472, GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid), 0.5);
	ElevatorBoostTimer = SetTimerEx("Elevator_Boost", 2000, 0, "i", floorid);
 	return 1;
}
stock RemoveFirstQueueFloor()
{
	for(new i; i < sizeof(ElevatorQueue) - 1; i ++)
	ElevatorQueue[i] = ElevatorQueue[i + 1];
	ElevatorQueue[sizeof(ElevatorQueue) - 1] = INVALID_FLOOR;
 	return 1;
}
stock AddFloorToQueue(floorid)
{
	new slot = -1;
	for(new i; i < sizeof(ElevatorQueue); i ++)
	{
		if(ElevatorQueue[i] == INVALID_FLOOR)
		{
			slot = i;
			break;
		}
	}
	if(slot != -1)
	{
		ElevatorQueue[slot] = floorid;
		if(ElevatorState == ELEVATOR_STATE_IDLE)
		ReadNextFloorInQueue();
  		return 1;
	}
 	return 0;
}
stock ResetElevatorQueue()
{
	for(new i; i < sizeof(ElevatorQueue); i ++)
	{
		ElevatorQueue[i] 	= INVALID_FLOOR;
		FloorRequestedBy[i] = INVALID_PLAYER_ID;
	}
 	return 1;
}
stock IsFloorInQueue(floorid)
{
	for(new i; i < sizeof(ElevatorQueue); i ++)
	if(ElevatorQueue[i] == floorid)
 	return 1;
 	return 0;
}
stock ReadNextFloorInQueue()
{
	if(ElevatorState != ELEVATOR_STATE_IDLE || ElevatorQueue[0] == INVALID_FLOOR)
 	return 0;
	Elevator_CloseDoors();
	Floor_CloseDoors(ElevatorFloor);
 	return 1;
}
forward Float:GetElevatorZCoordForFloor(floorid);
stock Float:GetElevatorZCoordForFloor(floorid)
return (GROUND_Z_COORD + FloorZOffsets[floorid] + ELEVATOR_OFFSET);
forward Float:GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid);
stock Float:GetDoorsZCoordForFloor(floorid)
return (GROUND_Z_COORD + FloorZOffsets[floorid]);
stock CallElevator(playerid, floorid)
{
	if(FloorRequestedBy[floorid] != INVALID_PLAYER_ID || IsFloorInQueue(floorid))
 	return 0;
	FloorRequestedBy[floorid] = playerid;
	AddFloorToQueue(floorid);
 	return 1;
}
stock DidPlayerRequestElevator(playerid)
{
	for(new i; i < sizeof(FloorRequestedBy); i ++)
	if(FloorRequestedBy[i] == playerid)
 	return 1;
 	return 0;
}
stock OnPlayerRegister(playerid, password[])
{
	new playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME+1], playerip[16], mquery[255];
	new day, month, year, string[12];
	getdate(year, month, day);
	GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
	GetPlayerIp(playerid, playerip, sizeof(playerip));
	format(string, sizeof(string), "%d/%d/%d", day, month, year);
	mysql_format(dbHandle, mquery, sizeof(mquery), "INSERT INTO accounts (name,password,Rip,Lip,Sex,Email,datereg) VALUES ('%e','%e','%s','%s',%d,'%e','%s')", playername, password, playerip, playerip, PlayerInfo[playerid][pSex], PlayerInfo[playerid][pEmail], string);
    mysql_query(dbHandle, mquery, false);
}
stock GetTimeAFK(playerid)
{
	new time = gettime()-active[playerid];
	return time;
}
stock BadFloat(Float:x)
{
	if(x >= 10.0 || x <= -10.0)
	return 1;

	return 0;
}
stock isNumeric(const string[])
{
	new length = strlen (string);
	if(length <= 0) return 0;
	for(new i = 0; i < length; i++)
	{
		if(
		(string[i] > '9' || string[i] < '0' && string[i]!='-' && string[i]!='+')
		|| (string[i]=='-' && i!=0)
		|| (string[i]=='+' && i!=0)
		) return 0;
	}
	if(length==1 && (string[0]=='-' || string[0]=='+')) return 0;
	return 1;
}
stock GetVehicleDriver(vehicleid)
{
	if(vehicleid < 1 || vehicleid > sizeof(VehicleDriverPlayerid)) return INVALID_PLAYER_ID; // invalid array
	if(VehicleDriverPlayerid[vehicleid - 1] != INVALID_PLAYER_ID  && IsPlayerInVehicle(VehicleDriverPlayerid[vehicleid - 1], vehicleid) && GetPlayerVehicleSeat(VehicleDriverPlayerid[vehicleid - 1]) == 0)
	return VehicleDriverPlayerid[vehicleid - 1]; // return playerid vehicledriver
	return VehicleDriverPlayerid[vehicleid - 1] = INVALID_PLAYER_ID;
}
stock strtok(const str[], &index,seperator=' ')
{
	new length = strlen(str);
	new offset = index;
	new result[128];
	while ((index < length) && (str[index] != seperator) && ((index - offset) < (sizeof(result) - 1)))
	{
		result[index - offset] = str[index];
		index++;
	}
	result[index - offset] = EOS;
	if((index < length) && (str[index] == seperator))
	{
		index++;
	}
	return result;
}
stock SpeedVehicle(playerid)
{
	new Float:PosX, Float:PosY, Float:PosZ, Float:PlayerSpeedDistance;
	GetVehicleVelocity(GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid), PosX, PosY, PosZ);
	PlayerSpeedDistance = floatmul(floatsqroot(floatadd(floatadd(floatpower(PosX, 2), floatpower(PosY, 2)), floatpower(PosZ, 2))), 170.0);
	new spe = floatround(PlayerSpeedDistance * 1);
	return spe;
}

stock SendPlaySound(soundid, Float:x, Float:y, Float:z)
{
    foreach(Player, i)
	{
		if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pMember] > 0 && PlayerInfo[i][pMember] <= 5)
			{
				PlayerPlaySound(i, soundid, Float:x, Float:y, Float:z);
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
}

stock SendRadioMessage(color, str[], radioid)
{
	foreach(Player, i)
	{
		if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pRadio] == radioid)
			{
				SendClientMessage(i, color, str);
			}
		}
	}
}
stock SMA(level, color, str[])
{
	for(new i = GetMaxPlayers()-1; i != -1; --i)
	{
		if(!IsPlayerConnected(i)) continue;
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] >= level)
			{
				SendClientMessage(i, color, str);
			}
		}
	}
}
stock SendAdminMessage(color, str[])
{
    foreach(Player, i)
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] >= 1)
		{
			SendClientMessage(i, color, str);
		}
	}
}

stock DicePlay(playerid)
{
    if(name_bone[playerid] < 999)
	{
		new dice = random(6)+1;
		new dice1 = random(6)+1;
		new diceplay = name_bone[playerid];
		new string[255];
  		format(string, sizeof(string), "%s и %s бросили кости. Результат: {CC9900}%i:%i",PlayerInfo[diceplay][pName],PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],dice,dice1);
		StatusMessage(playerid, string, "Играет в кости");
	}
}

stock IsGhettor(playerid)
{
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] >= 1 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] <= 5)
	{
		return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}
stock IsMhettor(playerid)
{
    if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] >= 10 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] <= 12)
    {
        return 1;
    }
    return 0;
}
stock ShowStats(playerid,statsid)
{
	if(login_check[statsid] == true)
	{
		new str[100],sctring[650];
		new status[15];
		switch(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLevel])
		{
		    case 0: {}
		    case 1: status = "Без статуса";
		    case 2..5: status = "Новичок";
		    case 6..9: status = "Развивающийся";
		    case 10..14: status = "Освоившийся";
		    case 15..19: status = "Опытный игрок";
		    case 20..29: status = "Активный игрок";
		    default: status = "Легендарный";
		}
		new sname[8];
		sname = (PlayerInfo[statsid][pSex] == 1) ? ("Мужской") : ("Женский");
		new nxtlevel = PlayerInfo[statsid][pLevel]+1;
		new slowpoke = nxtlevel*4;

		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Имя: {0099FF}\t\t\t\t%s\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pName]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Уровень: \t\t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pLevel]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Очки опыта: \t\t\t%i из %i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pCheckTime],slowpoke);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Номер телефона: \t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pPhone]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}На счету телефона: \t\t%i$\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pPhoneMoney]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Законопослушность: \t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pZakon]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Уровень розыска: \t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pWanted]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Уровень улучшений: \t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pUpdate]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Сила: \t\t\t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pSila]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Наркотики: \t\t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pDrugs]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Патроны: \t\t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pAmmo]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Металл: \t\t\t%d\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pMetal]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Маски: \t\t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pMask]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Аптечки: \t\t\t%i\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pHeal]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Пол: \t\t\t\t%s\n",sname);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pSex] == 1) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Женат на: \t\t\t%s\n\n\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pWedding]);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pSex] == 2) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Замужем за: \t\t\t%s\n\n\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pWedding]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pJob] == 0) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Организация: \t\t\t%s\n",GetGangName(PlayerInfo[statsid][pMember]));
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pJob] >= 1) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Работа: \t\t\t%s\n",GetJobName(PlayerInfo[statsid][pJob]));
		strcat(sctring,str);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pUnit] >= 1) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Подразделение: \t\t%s\n",GetUnitName(PlayerInfo[statsid][pMember], PlayerInfo[statsid][pUnit]));
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pUnit] >= 1) strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Должность: \t\t\t%s\n",RankName(statsid));
		strcat(sctring,str);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Ранг: \t\t\t\t%i\n\n\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pRang]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pHouse] == 999) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Проживание: \t\t\tБездомный\n");
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pHouse] < 999) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Проживание: \t\t\tДом №%d\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pHouse]);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pBusiness] == 999) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Бизнес: \t\t\tНет\n");
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pBusiness] < 999) format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Бизнес: \t\t\t№%d\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pBusiness]);
		format(str,sizeof(str),"{FFFFFF}Игровой статус: \t\t%s",status);
		strcat(sctring,str);
		if(PlayerInfo[statsid][pWarn] >= 1)
		{
			format(str,sizeof(str),"\n\n{FF6600}Предупреждения: \t\t%i из 3\n",PlayerInfo[statsid][pWarn]);
			strcat(sctring,str);
		}
		ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, 188, DIALOG_STYLE_MSGBOX, "{c69600}Статистика игрока", sctring, "", "Закрыть");
	}
}
stock IsABMX(playerid)
{
	new caridasd = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
	new model = GetVehicleModel(caridasd);
	if(model == 509 ||model == 481 || model == 510)
	{
		return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}
stock IsAir(playerid)
{
	new model = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
	if(model == AIRLS[0]||model == AIRLS[1]||model == AIRLS[2]||model == AIRLS[3]||model == AIRLS[4]||model == AIRLS[5]||model == AIRLS[6]||model == AIRLS[7])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}
stock IsBus(playerid)
{
	new model = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
	if(model== BUSLS[0]||model==BUSLS[1]||model==BUSLS[2]||model==BUSLS[3]||model==BUSLS[4]||model==BUSLS[5]||model==BUSLS[6]||model==BUSLS[7]||model==BUSLS[8]||model==BUSLS[9]||model==BUSLS[10])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	if(model==BUSLS[11]||model==BUSLS[12]||model==BUSLS[13]||model==BUSLS[14]||model==BUSLS[15]||model==BUSLS[16]||model==BUSLS[17])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	if(model==BUSSF[0]||model==BUSSF[1]||model==BUSSF[2]||model==BUSSF[3]||model==BUSSF[4]||model==BUSSF[5])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	if(model==BUSLV[0]||model==BUSLV[1]||model==BUSLV[2]||model==BUSLV[3]||model==BUSLV[4]||model==BUSLV[5]||model==BUSLV[6]||model==BUSLV[7]||model==BUSLV[8]||model==BUSLV[9]||model==BUSLV[10]||model==BUSLV[11]||model==BUSLV[12]||model==BUSLV[13]||model==BUSLV[14])
	{
		return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}

stock GetPlayerID(name[])
{
    foreach(new i : Player)
    {
        if(!strcmp(name, PlayerInfo[i][pName]))
            return i;
    }
    return -1;
}
stock PlayerToPoint(Float:radi, playerid, Float:xaxasasas, Float:y, Float:z)
{
	if(IsPlayerConnected(playerid))
	{
		new Float:oldposx, Float:oldposy, Float:oldposz;
		new Float:tempposx, Float:tempposy, Float:tempposz;
		GetPlayerPos(playerid, oldposx, oldposy, oldposz);
		tempposx = (oldposx -xaxasasas);
		tempposy = (oldposy -y);
		tempposz = (oldposz -z);
		if(((tempposx < radi) && (tempposx > -radi)) && ((tempposy < radi) && (tempposy > -radi)) && ((tempposz < radi) && (tempposz > -radi))) return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}
